Simple iterator type, to loop through each image of a list. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_ac4e7d5d973678ecd8250aa7eff9b9c98}{CImg\+List$<$\+T$>$\+::iterator}} type is defined as a {\ttfamily CImg$<$\+T$>$\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}.
\item You may use it like this\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a2d39db2f68af51153f623c43afc655a1}{CImgList<>}}\ list;\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Assuming\ this\ image\ list\ is\ not\ empty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a2d39db2f68af51153f623c43afc655a1}{CImgList<>::iterator}}\ it\ =\ list.begin();\ it<list.end();\ ++it)\ (*it).mirror(\textcolor{charliteral}{'x'});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Using the loop macro {\ttfamily cimglist\+\_\+for} is another (more concise) alternative\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{CImg_8h_ab0fbaf7f7ec6b68d1307757bf7285960}{cimglist\_for}}(list,l)\ list[l].mirror(\textcolor{charliteral}{'x'});}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{value\_type}{value\_type}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_ab3c229d5b1ee47f7c71cb1499b29e4e4} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
typedef T \mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{cimg\+\_\+library\+::\+CImg\+List}}$<$ T $>$\+::value\+\_\+type}



Pixel value type. 

Refer to the pixels value type of the images in the list. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_ab3c229d5b1ee47f7c71cb1499b29e4e4}{CImg\+List$<$\+T$>$\+::value\+\_\+type}} type of a {\ttfamily CImg\+List$<$\+T$>$} is defined to be a {\ttfamily T}. It is then similar to \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImg_a94119922993ffa72217a158fede82f3b}{CImg$<$\+T$>$\+::value\+\_\+type}.
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_ab3c229d5b1ee47f7c71cb1499b29e4e4}{CImg\+List$<$\+T$>$\+::value\+\_\+type}} is actually not used in CImg methods. It has been mainly defined for compatibility with STL naming conventions. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{cimg\+\_\+library\+::\+CImg\+List}}$<$ T $>$\+::\texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}\mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{CImg\+List}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Destructor. 

Destroy current list instance. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Any allocated buffer is deallocated.
\item Destroying an empty list does nothing actually. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\Hypertarget{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a2d39db2f68af51153f623c43afc655a1}\index{cimg\_library::CImgList$<$ T $>$@{cimg\_library::CImgList$<$ T $>$}!CImgList@{CImgList}}
\index{CImgList@{CImgList}!cimg\_library::CImgList$<$ T $>$@{cimg\_library::CImgList$<$ T $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CImgList()}{CImgList()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/20]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a2d39db2f68af51153f623c43afc655a1} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{cimg\+\_\+library\+::\+CImg\+List}}$<$ T $>$\+::\+CImg\+List (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Default constructor. 

Construct a new empty list instance. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item An empty list has no pixel data and its dimension \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_adaf35301d1cb3fd0b7f078c4d81c3f7e}{width()} is set to {\ttfamily 0}, as well as its image buffer pointer \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_ae822a6e8d2e98ef8e7d5a31499bc201b}{data()}.
\item An empty list may be reassigned afterwards, with the family of the \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a3432893660dfb114834cfbe2f06daec0}{assign()} methods. In all cases, the type of pixels stays {\ttfamily T}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a0f9c6c3ea20c2bb5c1efa312a718072e} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{cimg\+\_\+library\+::\+CImg\+List}}$<$ T $>$\+::\+CImg\+List (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a912c22174e375926e831f6b0b263bec9}{const}} unsigned int}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [explicit]}}



Construct list containing empty images. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & Number of empty images. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Useful when you know by advance the number of images you want to manage, as it will allocate the right amount of memory for the list, without needs for reallocation (that may occur when starting from an empty list and inserting several images in it). 
\end{DoxyNote}

Test if dimensions of each image of the list match specified arguments. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dx} & Checked image width. \\
\hline
{\em dy} & Checked image height. \\
\hline
{\em dz} & Checked image depth. \\
\hline
{\em dc} & Checked image spectrum. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Display the current \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{CImg\+List} instance in a new display window. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em disp} & Display window. \\
\hline
 & {\em display\+\_\+info} & Tells if image information are displayed on the standard output. \\
\hline
 & {\em axis} & Alignment axis for images viewing. \\
\hline
 & {\em align} & Appending alignment. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em XYZ} & Contains the XYZ coordinates at start / exit of the function. \\
\hline
 & {\em exit\+\_\+on\+\_\+anykey} & Exit function when any key is pressed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function opens a new window with a specific title and displays the list images of the current \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{CImg\+List} instance into it. Images of the list are appended in a single temporary image for visualization purposes. The function returns when a key is pressed or the display window is closed by the user. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Display the current \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{CImg\+List} instance in an existing CImg\+Display window (by reference). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em disp} & Reference to an existing CImg\+Display instance, where the current image list will be displayed. \\
\hline
{\em axis} & Appending axis. Can be {\ttfamily \{ \textquotesingle{}x\textquotesingle{} \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} \textquotesingle{}y\textquotesingle{} \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} \textquotesingle{}z\textquotesingle{} \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} \textquotesingle{}c\textquotesingle{} \}}. \\
\hline
{\em align} & Appending alignment. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function displays the list images of the current \doxylink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{CImg\+List} instance into an existing CImg\+Display window. Images of the list are appended in a single temporary image for visualization purposes. The function returns immediately. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Display a simple interactive interface to select images or sublists. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em disp} & Window instance to display selection and user interface. \\
\hline

\hline
{\em align} & Alignment setting when images have not all the same size. \\
\hline

\hline

Load an image from a video file, using Open\+CV library. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em filename} & Filename, as a C-\/string. \\
\hline
{\em first\+\_\+frame} & Index of the first frame to read. \\
\hline
{\em last\+\_\+frame} & Index of the last frame to read (can be higher than the actual number of frames, e.\+g. \textquotesingle{}\texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}0U\textquotesingle{}). \\
\hline
{\em step\+\_\+frame} & Step value for frame reading. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If step\+\_\+frame==0, the current video stream is forced to be released (without any frames read). 
\end{DoxyNote}

template$<$typename T$>$ \\
static \mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList_a912c22174e375926e831f6b0b263bec9}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcimg__library_1_1CImgList}{cimg\+\_\+library\+::\+CImg\+List}}$<$ T $>$\+::pixel\+\_\+type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



Return the type of image pixel values as a C string. 

Return a {\ttfamily char\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} string containing the usual type name of the image pixel values (i.\+e. a stringified version of the template parameter {\ttfamily T}). \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The returned string does not contain any spaces.
\item If the pixel type {\ttfamily T} does not correspond to a registered type, the string {\ttfamily "{}unknown"{}} is returned. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
